<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:философский.html>филосо́фский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">filosófskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> philosopher; philosopher's, philosophers'

<li>philosophic, philosophical</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:философствовать.html>филосо́фствующий</a> (20519)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:философствовать.html>филосо́фствующий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">filosófstvujuščij</span>)
</p>

***финал.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́л</a> (7312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finál</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>finale, ending, denouement
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:финал.html>фина́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выступление.html>выступле́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>был</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встреченный.html>встре́чен</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бурный.html>бу́рными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:овация.html>ова́циями</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Finál</b> jevó vystuplénija byl vstréčen búrnymi ovácijami.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">His performance ended in a standing ovation.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>final, final round</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">finanzieren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">financer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finansírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:финансировать.html>финанси́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">профинанси́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to finance, to fund</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ник</a> (25700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fínik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финик.html>фи́ников</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>date (fruit of the date palm)</li></ol>

***финишировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финишировать.html>финиши́ровать</a> (30636)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финиш.html>фи́ниш</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fíniš</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финишировать.html>финиши́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">finišírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to finish, to come in</li></ol>

***финка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:финка.html>фи́нка</a> (8777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финка.html>фи́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финка.html>фи́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финка.html>фи́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финка.html>фи́нок</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:финна.html>финн</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Finnish girl/woman (female person from Finland), female Finn</li>
<li>Finnish knife, puukko</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">финляндец</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">finljandec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">финляндка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">finljandka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a> (8795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фирма.html>фи́рма</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">fírma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fírmennyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фи́рменнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)фи́рменней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> firm, company, brand; proprietary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:блюдо.html>блю́до</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennoje</b> bljúdo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">house specialty</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>proprietary</b> dish</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:знак.html>знак</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> znak</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>proprietary</b> mark, trademark</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> sčót</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>company</b> account</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наименование.html>наименова́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennoje</b> naimenovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>brand</b> name</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:фирменный.html>фи́рменный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стиль.html>стиль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>fírmennyj</b> stilʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>corporate</b> style</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very good, high-quality</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:фишка.html>фи́шка</a> (18055)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">fiche</i>  + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фишка.html>фи́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">fíška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фи́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>фи́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:фишка.html>фи́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> piece, counter, dib, marker, peg, token</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> invention, contrivance, device, (funny or special) idea</li>

***флаг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:флаг.html>флаг</a> (3638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">vlag</i>.
